IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['α', 'β', 'β', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'α', 'α', 'α', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: α

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'α', 'α', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'α', 'α', 'β', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: α

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

Your Current Opinion: β

1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

Your Current Opinion: α

1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'α', 'β', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

Your Current Opinion: α

1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'β', 'α', 'α', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: α

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'β', 'α', 'α', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

Your Current Opinion: α

2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.

2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

After receiving the opinions of your friends, you must respond with the opinion you want to support.

IMPORTANT: Your response must contain ONLY the chosen opinion in square brackets - either [α] or [β].

You MUST choose either [α] or [β]. Your response must be ONLY [α] or [β] - nothing else.

Do not include any additional text, explanation, or formatting beyond the brackets and the letter.


=== USER PROMPT ===
Below you can see the complete list of opinions from all participants in your group, including your own.

Complete Opinion List: ['β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β', 'β']
Your Position: You are the opinion in the middle
Your Current Opinion: β

Here are the principles to follow when making your choice:
1. You must choose an opinion to support: either 'α' or 'β'
2. You should consider the opinions of all participants when making your choice
3. You can either keep your current opinion or change it based on the group

In all cases, respond ONLY with the chosen opinion in square brackets, for example: [α] or [β]

Reply only with the opinion you want to support, between square brackets [opinion].
